[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 1146002
     - Topic: Stress at work
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Stress at work

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]

```
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "STRESS_AT_WORK",
        "NAME": "Stress at Work Questionnaire",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,

          {
            "CODE": "Q1",
            "NAME": "Do you often feel overwhelmed by your workload?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Strongly Agree"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Agree"},
              {"ANSWER": "Neither Agree nor Disagree"},

              {"ANSWER": "Strongly Disagree"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q2",
            "NAME": "Do you feel like you're constantly putting out fires at work?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Strongly Agree"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Agree"},
              {"ANSWER": "Neither Agree nor Disagree"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Disagree"},
              {"ANSWER": "Strongly Disagree"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q3",
            "NAME": "Do you feel like you're not able to take breaks or step away from your work?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Strongly Agree"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Agree"},
              {"ANSWER": "Neither Agree nor Disagree"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Disagree"},
              {"ANSWER": "Strongly Disagree"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q4",
            "NAME": "Do you feel like your work is impacting your personal life?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Strongly Agree"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Agree"},
              {"ANSWER": "Neither Agree nor Disagree"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Disagree"},
              {"ANSWER": "Strongly Disagree"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q5",
            "NAME": "Do you feel like you're not able to manage your workload effectively?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Strongly Agree"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Agree"},
              {"ANSWER": "Neither Agree nor Disagree"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Disagree"},
              {"ANSWER": "Strongly Disagree"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q6",
            "NAME": "How would you rate your overall stress level at work?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 6,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Very High"},
              {"ANSWER": "High"},
              {"ANSWER": "Medium"},
              {"ANSWER": "Low"},
              {"ANSWER": "Very Low"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This questionnaire is designed to assess the level of stress an individual experiences at work. It includes a mix of questions that ask about the frequency and impact of stressors, as well as the individual's overall stress level. The answers are categorized into a 5-point Likert scale, with options ranging from "Strongly Agree" to "Strongly Disagree".

{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "WEPLACE",

              {"ANSWER": "Sometimes"},
              {"ANSWER": "Rarely"},
              {"ANSWER": "Never"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q3",
            "NAME": "How would you rate the cleanliness and organization of your workspace?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Excellent"},

              {"ANSWER": "Fair"},
              {"ANSWER": "Poor"},
              {"ANSWER": "Very poor"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q4",
            "NAME": "Do you have access to necessary resources and equipment to perform your job effectively?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes, always"},
              {"ANSWER": "Yes, most of the time"},
              {"ANSWER": "Sometimes"},
              {"ANSWER": "Rarely"},
              {"ANSWER": "Never"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q5",
            "NAME": "How would you rate the overall satisfaction with your workspace?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Very satisfied"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat satisfied"},
              {"ANSWER": "Neutral"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat dissatisfied"},
              {"ANSWER": "Very dissatisfied"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This questionnaire consists of 5 questions that assess the respondent's perception of their workplace environment. The questions cover aspects such as comfort, distractions, cleanliness, resources, and overall satisfaction. The answers are multiple-choice, with options ranging from "Very comfortable" to "Very dissatisfied".

            "TYPE_ID": 4,

              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}

              {"ANSWER": "Google Drive"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },

            "CODE": "Q7",

          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This questionnaire is designed to gather information about an individual's remote working experience, including their preferred remote work setup, frequency of remote work, and challenges faced while working remotely. It also asks about their prioritization of tasks, tools used for organization, and strategies for handling distractions. Finally, it asks about the most important aspect of remote work.

     - Topic: Manager feedback
     - Question number: 3
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Manager feedback

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation: Here is the generated questionnaire on Manager feedback in the specified JSON format:

```
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "MFB001",
        "NAME": "Manager Feedback Questionnaire",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "Q1",
            "NAME": "How would you rate your manager's overall performance?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Excellent"},
              {"ANSWER": "Good"},
              {"ANSWER": "Fair"},
              {"ANSWER": "Poor"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q2",
            "NAME": "What are your manager's greatest strengths?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Communication skills"},
              {"ANSWER": "Leadership abilities"},
              {"ANSWER": "Problem-solving skills"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q3",
            "NAME": "What areas would you like to see your manager improve?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Communication"},
              {"ANSWER": "Time management"},
              {"ANSWER": "Delegation"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q4",
            "NAME": "How would you rate your manager's ability to provide feedback and coaching?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [

              {"ANSWER": "Poor"}
            ]

              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}

      }
    ]
  }
}

            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.

The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.

```
{

    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {

        "NAME": "Employee Feedback Questionnaire",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "Q1",
            "NAME": "How satisfied are you with your current role?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Very Satisfied"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Satisfied"},
              {"ANSWER": "Neutral"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Dissatisfied"},
              {"ANSWER": "Very Dissatisfied"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q2",
            "NAME": "What do you like most about working for our organization?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Leadership"},
              {"ANSWER": "Colleagues"},
              {"ANSWER": "Work-Life Balance"},
              {"ANSWER": "Job Security"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q3",
            "NAME": "What do you think is the most significant challenge you face in your current role?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Lack of Resources"},
              {"ANSWER": "Insufficient Training"},
              {"ANSWER": "High Workload"},
              {"ANSWER": "Poor Communication"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q4",
            "NAME": "How would you rate the support you receive from your supervisor?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Excellent"},
              {"ANSWER": "Good"},
              {"ANSWER": "Fair"},
              {"ANSWER": "Poor"},
              {"ANSWER": "Very Poor"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q5",

            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes, I have a suggestion"},
              {"ANSWER": "No, I do not have a suggestion"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This questionnaire is designed to gather employee feedback on various aspects of their job, including job satisfaction, challenges, and supervisor support. [TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500000002
     - Topic: Employee experience
     - Question number: 16
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.

 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.

Generate me a questionnaire on Internal Mobility Opportunities

-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
Explanation: Here is the generated questionnaire on Internal Mobility Opportunities in JSON format:

```
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "IMOBILITY",
        "NAME": "Internal Mobility Opportunities",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "Q1",
            "NAME": "Have you considered exploring internal mobility opportunities within the company?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes, I'm interested in exploring internal mobility opportunities."},
              {"ANSWER": "No, I'm not interested in exploring internal mobility opportunities."}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q2",
            "NAME": "What motivates you to consider internal mobility opportunities?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "New challenges and opportunities"},
              {"ANSWER": "Career growth and development"},
              {"ANSWER": "Better work-life balance"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q3",
            "NAME": "What internal mobility opportunities would you like to explore?",
            "TYPE_ID": 6,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Role changes"},
              {"ANSWER": "Department transfers"},
              {"ANSWER": "Location changes"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q4",
            "NAME": "What barriers do you face in exploring internal mobility opportunities?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Lack of information about opportunities"},
              {"ANSWER": "Fear of change"},
              {"ANSWER": "Concerns about job security"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q5",
            "NAME": "How important is internal mobility to you?",
            "TYPE_ID": 8,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 5,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Very important"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat important"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not very important"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not at all important"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

It covers topics such as motivation, desired opportunities, and perceived barriers. The questionnaire is designed to be engaging and easy to understand, with a mix of single-answer and multiple-answer questions.

Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Internal Mobility Opportunities

-------------------
-------------------

```
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "IMOO",
        "NAME": "Internal Mobility Opportunities",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "Q1",
            "NAME": "Have you considered exploring internal mobility opportunities within the company?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Yes"},
              {"ANSWER": "No"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q2",
            "NAME": "What motivates you to consider internal mobility opportunities?",
            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Career growth"},
              {"ANSWER": "New challenges"},
              {"ANSWER": "Better work-life balance"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q3",
            "NAME": "How important is internal mobility to you?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Very important"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat important"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not very important"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not at all important"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q4",
            "NAME": "What would make you more likely to consider internal mobility opportunities?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,

            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.

 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.

 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.

 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "Very Effective"},
              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Effective"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not Very Effective"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not at All Effective"}
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q2",
            "NAME": "What did you enjoy most about the teambuilding initiative?",
            "TYPE_ID": 1,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {"ANSWER": "The teambuilding activities"},
              {"ANSWER": "The opportunity to bond with colleagues"},
              {"ANSWER": "The food and refreshments"},
              {"ANSWER": "Other (please specify)"}
            ]
          },

            "CODE": "Q3",

            "TYPE_ID": 2,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [

              {"ANSWER": "The teambuilding activities were not relevant to our work"},

            ]

              {"ANSWER": "Somewhat Likely"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not Very Likely"},
              {"ANSWER": "Not at All Likely"}
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}

This questionnaire is designed to gather feedback on the effectiveness of a teambuilding initiative. It includes four questions:

1. How would you rate the overall effectiveness of the teambuilding initiative? (Rating scale: Very Effective, Somewhat Effective, Not Very Effective, Not at All Effective)
2. What did you enjoy most about the teambuilding initiative? (Multiple-choice question with options: The teambuilding activities, The opportunity to bond with colleagues, The food and refreshments, Other (please specify))
3. What did you find most challenging or frustrating about the teambuilding initiative? (Multiple-choice question with options: The activities were too structured, The teambuilding activities were not relevant to our work, The food and refreshments were not satisfactory, Other (please specify))
4. How likely are you to recommend this teambuilding initiative to your colleagues? (Rating scale: Very Likely, Somewhat Likely, Not Very Likely, Not at All Likely)

This questionnaire aims to gather feedback on the effectiveness of the teambuilding initiative, what aspects were enjoyed or found challenging, and whether participants would recommend the initiative to others.

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.
The user will ask you to generate a questionnaire about a specified topic.
Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
Think about the questionnaire content step by step.

            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.

You are a Questionnaire Generator in the Human Resource Management field.

Firstly describe how the questionnaire is structured. Start with 'Explanation: '. Then format the questionnaire as a JSON, which must respect the following format:
 - The root of the JSON is an object that contains a single property 'data'.
        - The 'data' property is an object that contains a single property 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES'.
        - 'TF_QUESTIONNAIRES' is an array of only one element, which represents a questionnaire. It has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the questionnaire's code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the questionnaire's name.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) which is equal to 3.
            - '_TF_QUESTIONS': An array of objects, each representing a question.
        - Each question in the '_TF_QUESTIONS' array has the following properties:
            - 'CODE': (string) the question's unique code.
            - 'NAME': (string) the question's content.
            - 'TYPE_ID': (int) the question's type.
            - 'DISPLAY_ORDER': (int) the question's display order.
            - '_TF_ANSWERS': An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.
        - Each answer object in the '_TF_ANSWERS' array has a single property 'ANSWER', which is a string representing the content of the answer.
The admitted question's types are the following:
 - ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
 - ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one or more answer from a list.
 - ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something.
 - ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to aquire feedback.
 - ID: 5, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to reorder items.
 - ID: 6, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to disribute weights across several items/options.
 - ID: 7, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to clone questions from a template.
 - ID: 8, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question when the answer to be given is a date or a date/time.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement.
